            <!---->
            <h6 _ngcontent-c126="">SYLLABUS</h6>
            <h2 _ngcontent-c126="" class="h3">Become a Machine Learning Engineer</h2>
            <p _ngcontent-c126="" class="small hidden-md-down">In this program, you will master the skills necessary to become a successful Machine Learning Engineer. You will build effective machine learning models, and learn to approach and solve real-world problems across a wide array of fields.</p>
            <p _ngcontent-c126="" class="small hidden-lg-up">Become a Machine Learning Engineer. Master skills by building models that solve real-world challenges.</p>
            <!---->
            <!---->
            <!---->
            <div _ngcontent-c126="" class="nd-syllabus-term__header__content--details">
             <p _ngcontent-c126="" class="nd-syllabus-term__toggle text-only">
              <!---->
              <!----><span _ngcontent-c126="">See fewer details</span></p>
             <!---->
             <p _ngcontent-c126="" class="x-small gray-medium hidden-md-down">6 months to complete </p>
            </div>
           </div>

              <section _ngcontent-c148="" class="degree-syllabus-preview__content--parts">
               <!---->
               <!---->
               <!---->
               <ul _ngcontent-c148="">
                <!---->
                <li _ngcontent-c148="">
                 <div _ngcontent-c148="" class="part">
                  <!---->
                  <h4 _ngcontent-c148="" class="h5 mb-half">Machine Learning Foundations</h4>
                  <p _ngcontent-c148="" class="small mb-half">Explore the core concepts of Machine Learning which involve understanding the nuances in your data.</p>
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <span _ngcontent-c148="" class="part__project text-only"><img _ngcontent-c148="" class="icon-middle" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-project.svg"><span _ngcontent-c148="">Predicting Boston Housing Prices</span></span>
                  <!---->
                 </div></li>
                <li _ngcontent-c148="">
                 <div _ngcontent-c148="" class="part">
                  <!---->
                  <h4 _ngcontent-c148="" class="h5 mb-half">Supervised Learning</h4>
                  <p _ngcontent-c148="" class="small mb-half">Now that you have a background in model building, you will learn about supervised learning, a common class of methods for model construction.</p>
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <span _ngcontent-c148="" class="part__project text-only"><img _ngcontent-c148="" class="icon-middle" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-project.svg"><span _ngcontent-c148="">Find Donors for CharityML</span></span>
                  <!---->
                 </div></li>
                <li _ngcontent-c148="">
                 <div _ngcontent-c148="" class="part">
                  <!---->
                  <h4 _ngcontent-c148="" class="h5 mb-half">Unsupervised Learning</h4>
                  <p _ngcontent-c148="" class="small mb-half">In this lesson, we will cover unsupervised learning and how it is suitable for different kinds of problem domains.</p>
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <span _ngcontent-c148="" class="part__project text-only"><img _ngcontent-c148="" class="icon-middle" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-project.svg"><span _ngcontent-c148="">Creating Customer Segments</span></span>
                  <!---->
                 </div></li>
                <li _ngcontent-c148="">
                 <div _ngcontent-c148="" class="part">
                  <!---->
                  <h4 _ngcontent-c148="" class="h5 mb-half">Deep Learning</h4>
                  <p _ngcontent-c148="" class="small mb-half">In this lesson, well cover topics in Deep Learning including Convolutional Neural Networks.</p>
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <span _ngcontent-c148="" class="part__project text-only"><img _ngcontent-c148="" class="icon-middle" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-project.svg"><span _ngcontent-c148="">Dog Breed Classifier</span></span>
                  <!---->
                 </div></li>
                <li _ngcontent-c148="">
                 <div _ngcontent-c148="" class="part">
                  <!---->
                  <h4 _ngcontent-c148="" class="h5 mb-half">Reinforcement Learning</h4>
                  <p _ngcontent-c148="" class="small mb-half">In this lesson, we'll cover topics in Reinforcement Learning like Markov Decision Processes, Monte Carlo methods and Temporal Difference methods.</p>
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <span _ngcontent-c148="" class="part__project text-only"><img _ngcontent-c148="" class="icon-middle" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-project.svg"><span _ngcontent-c148="">Train a quadcopter how to fly</span></span>
                  <!---->
                 </div></li>
                <li _ngcontent-c148="">
                 <div _ngcontent-c148="" class="part">
                  <!---->
                  <h4 _ngcontent-c148="" class="h5 mb-half">Capstone Project</h4>
                  <p _ngcontent-c148="" class="small mb-half">This section has two phases. The first is the Capstone Proposal, during which you will draft a proposal outlining the domain of the problem you would like to solve, and your approach. This is followed by the Capstone Project: Here, you will leverage your newly-learned skills to solve the problemas outlined in your proposalby applying machine learning algorithms and techniques.</p>
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <!---->
                  <span _ngcontent-c148="" class="part__project text-only"><img _ngcontent-c148="" class="icon-middle" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-project.svg"><span _ngcontent-c148="">CAPSTONE PROPOSAL</span></span>
                  <span _ngcontent-c148="" class="part__project text-only"><img _ngcontent-c148="" class="icon-middle" src="/assets/iridium/images/nanodegree-overview/shared/degree-syllabus/icon-project.svg"><span _ngcontent-c148="">CAPSTONE PROJECT</span></span>
                  <!---->
                 </div></li>

Including:<ul><li>Populations, samples</li><li>Mean, median, mode</li><li>Standard error</li><li>Variation, standard deviations</li><li>Normal distribution</li><li>Precision and accuracy<br><br></li></ul></li><li><strong>Intermediate calculus and linear algebra mastery</strong>, addressed in the <a href=&quot;https://www.udacity.com/course/linear-algebra-refresher-course--ud953&quot;>Linear Algebra Refresher Course</a>, including:<ul><li>Derivatives</li><li>Integrals</li><li>Series expansions</li><li>Matrix operations through eigenvectors and eigenvalues</li></ul></li></ul><p><strong><em>We have compiled additional resources for preparation <a href=&quot;https://www.udacity.com/wiki/nd009?nocache#!#preliminary-resources&quot;>here</a>.</em></strong></p>">
                 <p>Prior to entering the Machine Learning Engineer Nanodegree program, the student should have the following knowledge:</p>
                 <ul>
                  <li><strong>Intermediate Python programming knowledge</strong>, of the sort gained through the <a href="https://www.udacity.com/course/intro-to-programming-nanodegree--nd000">Introduction to Programming Nanodegree</a>, other introductory programming courses or programs, or additional real-world software development experience. Including:
                   <ul>
                    <li>Strings, numbers, and variables</li>

                   </ul></li>

        <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="faq__content">
         <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="faq__header">
          <h4 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h2">
           <!---->FAQ</h4>
          <!---->
          <!---->
          <!---->
         </div>
         <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="more fade">
          <div _ngcontent-c49="">
           <!---->
           <ul _ngcontent-c49="" class="faq__list">
            <!---->
            <h5 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h3">HIGHLIGHTS</h5>
            <!---->
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Why should I enroll in the Machine Learning Nanodegree Program?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="Machine learning is everywhere, and is often at work even when we don't realize it. Google Translate, Siri, and Facebook News Feeds are just a few popular examples of machine learning's omnipresence. The ability to develop machines and systems that can automatically improve themselves puts machine learning at the absolute forefront of virtually any field that relies on data. If you are interested in the field of Machine Learning, and want to get hands on experience building models to topical datasets, so that you can join the pioneers who lead this field in the industry today, this program is ideal.<br><br>This program is also excellent for Data Analysts who want to move into a more machine learning centric role because this program focuses specifically on building real world skills that you will be able to apply to your Machine Learning Engineer job. The goal of the Machine Learning Nanodegree program is to equip you with key skills that will prepare you to fill roles within companies seeking machine learning experts as well as those looking to introduce machine learning techniques to their organizations. Those skills cover Supervised Learning, Unsupervised Learning, Reinforcement Learning, and Deep Learning.">
              Machine learning is everywhere, and is often at work even when we don't realize it. Google Translate, Siri, and Facebook News Feeds are just a few popular examples of machine learning's omnipresence. The ability to develop machines and systems that can automatically improve themselves puts machine learning at the absolute forefront of virtually any field that relies on data. If you are interested in the field of Machine Learning, and want to get hands on experience building models to topical datasets, so that you can join the pioneers who lead this field in the industry today, this program is ideal.
              <br>
              <br>This program is also excellent for Data Analysts who want to move into a more machine learning centric role because this program focuses specifically on building real world skills that you will be able to apply to your Machine Learning Engineer job. The goal of the Machine Learning Nanodegree program is to equip you with key skills that will prepare you to fill roles within companies seeking machine learning experts as well as those looking to introduce machine learning techniques to their organizations. Those skills cover Supervised Learning, Unsupervised Learning, Reinforcement Learning, and Deep Learning.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Where can I find the syllabus for this course?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="Please <a href=&quot;https://s3-us-west-1.amazonaws.com/udacity-content/PDFs/Syllabus-MachineLearningNanodegree.pdf&quot;>take a look</a>.">
              Please 
              <a href="https://s3-us-west-1.amazonaws.com/udacity-content/PDFs/Syllabus-MachineLearningNanodegree.pdf">take a look</a>.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Will content from the program also be available for free outside of the Nanodegree program?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="While some of the video material is available outside of the program, most of the material will only be available to currently enrolled Nanodegree students. Access to project feedback, instructor support, and hiring partners are benefits exclusive to the Nanodegree programs.">
              While some of the video material is available outside of the program, most of the material will only be available to currently enrolled Nanodegree students. Access to project feedback, instructor support, and hiring partners are benefits exclusive to the Nanodegree programs.
             </div></li>
           </ul>
           <ul _ngcontent-c49="" class="faq__list">
            <!---->
            <h5 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h3">FEE AND PAYMENTS</h5>
            <!---->
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">How much does the Nanodegree program cost?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="This Nanodegree program consists of one term that is six months long. Students must complete the full six months to earn their credential and graduate. The term costs 999&amp;#8364;, which is paid at the beginning of the term. (Fee and currency are shown based on your location.)">
              This Nanodegree program consists of one term that is six months long. Students must complete the full six months to earn their credential and graduate. The term costs 999, which is paid at the beginning of the term. (Fee and currency are shown based on your location.)
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Is there a free trial period for this program?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="No, there is no free trial period for this program.">
              No, there is no free trial period for this program.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">What is the refund policy?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="There is a 7-day refund policy. During this time, you can visit the Settings page of your Udacity classroom where you can unenroll and request a full refund. This 7-day window begins the day the classroom opens. After the first 7 days, course fees are non-refundable.">
              There is a 7-day refund policy. During this time, you can visit the Settings page of your Udacity classroom where you can unenroll and request a full refund. This 7-day window begins the day the classroom opens. After the first 7 days, course fees are non-refundable.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Are there any scholarships available for this program?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="All current scholarship opportunities are posted on <a href=&quot;https://www.udacity.com/scholarships&quot;>our scholarships page</a>.">
              All current scholarship opportunities are posted on 
              <a href="https://www.udacity.com/scholarships">our scholarships page</a>.
             </div></li>
           </ul>
           <ul _ngcontent-c49="" class="faq__list">
            <!---->
            <h5 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h3">STRUCTURE</h5>
            <!---->
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">What is a Nanodegree Program?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="To read more about our Nanodegree program structure, please refer to <a href=&quot;https://udacity.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/207694976-What-is-a-Nanodegree-program-What-s-the-experience-like-&quot;>Udacity FAQ</a>.">
              To read more about our Nanodegree program structure, please refer to 
              <a href="https://udacity.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/207694976-What-is-a-Nanodegree-program-What-s-the-experience-like-">Udacity FAQ</a>.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Is this program online, in-person, or some combination of both?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="The program is online, and students interact with peers, mentors, coaches, and instructors in our virtual classrooms, in forums, and on Slack.">
              The program is online, and students interact with peers, mentors, coaches, and instructors in our virtual classrooms, in forums, and on Slack.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Is this program self-paced?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="It is not. This is a unique, termed program that requires students to keep pace with their peers throughout the duration of the program. If a student does not complete a term by the term deadline, they will be removed from the program and will need to re-enroll in a new term and pay the full term fee in order to continue.">
              It is not. This is a unique, termed program that requires students to keep pace with their peers throughout the duration of the program. If a student does not complete a term by the term deadline, they will be removed from the program and will need to re-enroll in a new term and pay the full term fee in order to continue.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Can I enroll in the program at any time?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="Yes! We admit students on a rolling basis, and you will automatically be added to the next available term once you've successfully enrolled. Every term has a fixed start date, and content becomes available on that date.">
              Yes! We admit students on a rolling basis, and you will automatically be added to the next available term once you've successfully enrolled. Every term has a fixed start date, and content becomes available on that date.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Can I enter the classroom prior to the start of my term?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="Yes, but you won't be able to access the content, as it stays locked until your term begins. In the classroom, you'll see a countdown to your term's start date.">
              Yes, but you won't be able to access the content, as it stays locked until your term begins. In the classroom, you'll see a countdown to your term's start date.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">What happens if I don't complete a project on time?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="It is strongly recommended that you complete each project on time to ensure you meet graduation requirements. To graduate, you must complete, submit, and meet expectations for all required projects within four months of your start date. While there is no penalty for missing a project deadline, missing one puts you at risk to be removed from the program if you do not stay on track and complete all required projects before the term ends. Finally, by keeping pace with your fellow students, you'll gain much more value from forums and Slack channels!">
              It is strongly recommended that you complete each project on time to ensure you meet graduation requirements. To graduate, you must complete, submit, and meet expectations for all required projects within four months of your start date. While there is no penalty for missing a project deadline, missing one puts you at risk to be removed from the program if you do not stay on track and complete all required projects before the term ends. Finally, by keeping pace with your fellow students, you'll gain much more value from forums and Slack channels!
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">What happens if I don't complete a term by the term deadline?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="You will receive a free four-week extension, which is automatically applied to your account if you do not complete the term within the allotted six-month timeframe. If you do not complete the term within the extension, you will be removed from the program and will no longer be able to access course content. To resume access to the course, you would need to pay the term fee again. Your progress would carry over, so you would be able to continue where you left off.">
              You will receive a free four-week extension, which is automatically applied to your account if you do not complete the term within the allotted six-month timeframe. If you do not complete the term within the extension, you will be removed from the program and will no longer be able to access course content. To resume access to the course, you would need to pay the term fee again. Your progress would carry over, so you would be able to continue where you left off.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Will I be able to pause or defer my Nanodegree program?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="No. Due to the fixed-term nature of the Machine Learning Nanodegree program, and the need for maintaining a consistent and stable student body throughout, it will not be possible to pause or defer your enrollment in this program. We ask that you please make sure to enroll for a term only if you are able to commit to the entire time frame.">
              No. Due to the fixed-term nature of the Machine Learning Nanodegree program, and the need for maintaining a consistent and stable student body throughout, it will not be possible to pause or defer your enrollment in this program. We ask that you please make sure to enroll for a term only if you are able to commit to the entire time frame.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Will I have access to the material even after the term ends?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="No. You will retain access to the program materials for a period of time after graduation and you may download certain materials for your own records if you wish. Please note however, that students who leave the program&amp;#8212;or who are removed from the program for failure to meet deadlines&amp;#8212;prior to successfully graduating, will cease to have access.">
              No. You will retain access to the program materials for a period of time after graduation and you may download certain materials for your own records if you wish. Please note however, that students who leave the programor who are removed from the program for failure to meet deadlinesprior to successfully graduating, will cease to have access.
             </div></li>
           </ul>
           <ul _ngcontent-c49="" class="faq__list">

            <h5 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h3">PREREQUISITES</h5>

            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">What software and versions will I need in this program?</h6>

              We recommend having Anaconda installed with Python 2.7 as a minimum. Virtually any 64-bit operating with at least 8GB of RAM will be suitable.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Is payment due before the term begins?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="Yes. In this way, we know exactly how many student are in a term, and can optimize our instructional and support resources accordingly. Additionally, this approach ensures a consistent and stable student body throughout the program, which fosters a deeper sense of community, and enables richer collaborations as students work together as a group.">
              Yes. In this way, we know exactly how many student are in a term, and can optimize our instructional and support resources accordingly. Additionally, this approach ensures a consistent and stable student body throughout the program, which fosters a deeper sense of community, and enables richer collaborations as students work together as a group.
             </div></li>
            <li _ngcontent-c49=""><h6 _ngcontent-c49="" class="h4">Can I enroll in other Nanodegree programs while I'm enrolled in the Machine Learning Nanodegree program?</h6>
             <!---->
             <div _ngcontent-c49="" class="answer-content" innerhtml="Our programs require a serious time commitment from students, so while we do not recommend doing so, we do not prohibit concurrent enrollments. This is an intensive, paced program, and students must proceed throughout the programs at the required rate of progress. To make the most of your experience, we believe you are best served by focusing on one program at a time and being fully immersed in the unique structure and pacing. You can always take one after the other!">
              Our programs require a serious time commitment from students, so while we do not recommend doing so, we do not prohibit concurrent enrollments. This is an intensive, paced program, and students must proceed throughout the programs at the required rate of progress. To make the most of your experience, we believe you are best served by focusing on one program at a time and being fully immersed in the unique structure and pacing. You can always take one after the other!
             </div></li>
           </ul>

You will also complete a capstone project in your chosen domain.&q;,&q;slug&q;:&q;machine-learning-engineer-nanodegree--nd009&q;,&q;starter&q;:false,&q;student_groups&q;:[&q;5783912581955584&q;,&q;5807803480145920&q;,&q;5270207414927360&q;,&q;4690496762675200&q;,&q;5081227872436224&q;,&q;5319291655946240&q;,&q;6066628850352128&q;,&q;5590634796417024&q;,&q;5005136415686656&q;,&q;6095420591439872&q;,&q;5400542882562048&q;,&q;5871573019656192&q;,&q;6065194831446016&q;,&q;5583925651701760&q;,&q;5008831690833920&q;,&q;6182998238822400&q;,&q;5398639458123776&q;,&q;6193470669324288&q;,&q;5509474824224768&q;,&q;4844724079558656&q;,&q;5144523752341504&q;,&q;6515371784536064&q;,&q;6217236604518400&q;,&q;5527193434980352&q;,&q;5975056925327360&q;,&q;6216342131441664&q;,&q;5345768759361536&q;,&q;bd-nd009-students&q;],&q;subtitle&q;:&q;Supervised Learning, Unsupervised Learning, Reinforcement Learning, and Deep Learning.&q;,&q;summary&q;:&q;In this program you will master Supervised, Unsupervised, Reinforcement, and Deep Learning fundamentals. You will also complete a capstone project in your chosen domain.&q;,&q;syllabus&q;:&q;&l;p&g;As a student in the Machine Learning Nanodegree program, you will build the  projects listed below. Each project has a &l;strong&g;supporting course&l;/strong&g;. Reviewers will provide feedback on your projects and guidance on how to take your project to the next level.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;p&g;&l;em&g;Note: Unless otherwise mentioned in the individual project descriptions, you will need to implement your projects in *&l;/em&g;Python 2.7&l;strong&g;. Familiarity with numerical and scientific computing libraries like **NumPy&l;/strong&g; and &l;strong&g;SciPy&l;/strong&g; will be very helpful.*&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Project 0: Titanic Survival Exploration (Optional)&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;In this project, you will create decision functions that attempt to predict survival outcomes from the 1912 Titanic disaster based on each passengers features, such as sex and age. You will start with a simple algorithm and increase its complexity until you are able to accurately predict the outcomes for at least 80% of the passengers in the provided data. This project will introduce you to some of the concepts of machine learning as you start the Nanodegree program.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;p&g;&l;strong&g;&l;em&g;The supporting course covers:&l;/em&g;&l;/strong&g; Introduction to Artificial Intelligence and Machine Learning.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Project 1: Predicting Boston Housing Prices&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;You want to be the best real estate agent out there. In order to compete with other agents in your area, you decide to use machine learning. You are going to use various statistical analysis tools to build the best model to predict the value of a given house. Your task is to find the best price your client can sell their house at. The best guess from a model is one that best generalizes the data.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;p&g;&l;strong&g;&l;em&g;The supporting course covers:&l;/em&g;&l;/strong&g;  Statistics Review &a;amp; Supporting Libraries, Evaluating Model Performance, Model Evaluation &a;amp; Validation, and Model Optimization.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Project 2: Finding Donors for CharityML&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;CharityML, a fictitious charity organization, has brought you on board to help build an algorithm to best identify potential donors and reduce overhead cost of sending mail. Your goal will be evaluate and optimize several different supervised learners to determine which algorithm will provide the highest donation yield while also reducing the total number of letters being sent.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;p&g;&l;strong&g;&l;em&g;The supporting course covers:&l;/em&g;&l;/strong&g;  Supervised Learning Intro, Decision Trees, Regression, Neural Networks, Kernel Methods, Instance Based Learning, Bayesian Learning, Ensemble Learning.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Project 3: Creating Customer Segments&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;A wholesale distributor is looking to optimize their delivery methods, and has reached out to you for help. In this project, you will be given unstructured data about the customers. You will then use unsupervised learning techniques to find similarities between them, segment them into distinct categories, and finally recommend the best delivery service for each cluster of customers.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;p&g;&l;strong&g;&l;em&g;The supporting course covers:&l;/em&g;&l;/strong&g;   Clustering, Feature Scaling, Feature Selection, Feature Transformation, Semi-Supervised Learning.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Project 4: Train a Smartcab to Drive&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;A smartcab is a self-driving car from the not-so-distant future that ferries people from one arbitrary location to another. In this project, you will use reinforcement learning to train a smartcab how to drive in real-time, optimizing for both safety and efficiency.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;p&g;&l;strong&g;&l;em&g;The supporting course covers:&l;/em&g;&l;/strong&g;  Markov Decision Processes, Reinforcement Learning, and Game Theory.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Project 5: Build a Digit Recognition Program&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;In this project, you will create a live camera application or program that prints numbers it observes in real time from images it is given, using what you&a;#39;ve learned about deep neural networks and convolutional neural networks.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;p&g;&l;strong&g;&l;em&g;The supporting course covers:&l;/em&g;&l;/strong&g;  Deep Neural Networks, Convolutional Neural Networks.&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;h3&g;Project 6: Capstone Project&l;/h3&g;\n\n&l;p&g;In this capstone project, you will leverage what youve learned throughout the Nanodegree program to solve a problem of your choice by applying machine learning algorithms and techniques. You will first &l;strong&g;define&l;/strong&g; the problem you want to solve and investigate potential solutions and performance metrics. Next, you will &l;strong&g;analyze&l;/strong&g; the problem through visualizations and data exploration to have a better understanding of what algorithms and features are appropriate for solving it. You will then &l;strong&g;implement&l;/strong&g; your algorithms and metrics of choice, documenting the preprocessing, refinement, and postprocessing steps along the way. Afterwards, you will collect &l;strong&g;results&l;/strong&g; about the performance of the models used, visualize significant quantities, and validate/justify these values. Finally, you will construct &l;strong&g;conclusions&l;/strong&g; about your results, and discuss whether your implementation adequately solves the problem. Suggested application areas include:&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;ul&g;\n&l;li&g;Deep Learning&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g;Robot Motion Planning&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g;Healthcare&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g;Education&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g;Computer Vision&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g;Investment and Trading&l;/li&g;\n&l;/ul&g;\n\n&l;h2&g;Want a preview?&l;/h2&g;\n\n&l;p&g;We have selected and compiled content for this program from the following free courses:&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;p&g;&l;strong&g;General:&l;/strong&g;&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;ul&g;\n&l;li&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.udacity.com/course/intro-to-machine-learning--ud120\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;Udacity&a;#39;s Introduction to Machine Learning&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g; &l;a href=\&q;https://www.udacity.com/course/knowledge-based-ai-cognitive-systems--ud409\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;Georgia Tech&a;#39;s Knowledge-based AI&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.udacity.com/course/intro-to-data-analysis--ud170\&q;&g;Udacity&a;#39;s Introduction to Data Analysis&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g; &l;a href=\&q;https://www.udacity.com/course/machine-learning--ud262\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;Georgia Tech&a;#39;s Machine Learning&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n&l;/ul&g;\n\n&l;p&g;&l;strong&g;Specific to Project 1:&l;/strong&g;&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;ul&g;\n&l;li&g; &l;a href=\&q;https://www.udacity.com/course/intro-to-data-science--ud359\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;Udacity&a;#39;s Introduction to Data Science&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n&l;li&g; &l;a href=\&q;https://www.udacity.com/course/intro-to-descriptive-statistics--ud827\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;Udacity&a;#39;s Descriptive Statistics&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n&l;/ul&g;\n\n&l;p&g;&l;strong&g;Specific to Project 4:&l;/strong&g;&l;/p&g;\n\n&l;ul&g;\n&l;li&g; &l;a href=\&q;https://www.udacity.com/course/reinforcement-learning--ud600\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;Georgia Tech&a;#39;s Reinforcement Learning&l;/a&g;&l;/li&g;\n&l;/ul&g;\n\n&l;p&g;&l;em&g;Our free content maintains the same high level of quality as our Nanodegree course material. However, it is only through enrollment in a Nanodegree program that you receive direct mentoring, benefit from our best-in-class personal code review system, have the opportunity to submit your work for review, and earn industry-designed and recognized
